1 billion views? wtf
For those not in the know, this viewcount was caused by a little bit of what I presume was a programming error. Essentially, the the app and webapp, when you first opened the Lootboxes tab, it played this video. However, when minimized, the iframe (basically just a window that displays another page) would auto-play and loop the same video over and over again, and since a lot of people spent multiple minutes in that tab, it constantly added a new view every time the video was played.
